<h3 class='post-title entry-title' itemprop='name'>

</div>
<div class='post-body entry-content' id='post-body-8939608206300647885' itemprop='description articleBody'>

<i><span style="color: #45818e; font-family: &quot;trebuchet ms&quot; , sans-serif; font-size: large;">Sans unwarranted expense</span></i><br />

<h2 class='date-header'><span>15.2.16</span></h2>

          <div class="date-posts">
        
<div class='post-outer'>
<div class='post hentry uncustomized-post-template' itemprop='blogPost' itemscope='itemscope' itemtype='http://schema.org/BlogPosting'>
<meta content='https://4.bp.blogspot.com/-cWqqhNWc1A8/VsCtJGcZESI/AAAAAAAABM4/rHYf69-ZGic/s400/Antonin_Scalia%252C_SCOTUS_photo_portrait%2B-%2BPENCIL.jpg' itemprop='image_url'/>
<meta content='275300702743490151' itemprop='blogId'/>
<meta content='4443514259317132751' itemprop='postId'/>
<a name='4443514259317132751'></a>
<h3 class='post-title entry-title' itemprop='name'>
<a href='http://daikupcj.blogspot.com/2016/02/unconsidered-opinion.html'>Unconsidered Opinion</a>
</h3>
<div class='post-header'>
<div class='post-header-line-1'></div>
</div>
<div class='post-body entry-content' id='post-body-4443514259317132751' itemprop='description articleBody'>
<i><span style="color: #674ea7; font-family: &quot;helvetica neue&quot; , &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif; font-size: large;">Antonin Scalia</span></i><br />
<i><span style="color: #674ea7; font-family: &quot;helvetica neue&quot; , &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif; font-size: large;">Inter alia</span></i><br />
<i><span style="color: #674ea7; font-family: &quot;helvetica neue&quot; , &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif; font-size: large;">Expressed his dissent</span></i><br />
<i><span style="color: #674ea7; font-family: &quot;helvetica neue&quot; , &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif; font-size: large;">From that last judgment</span></i><br />
<i><span style="color: #45818e; font-family: &quot;trebuchet ms&quot; , sans-serif; font-size: large;"><br /></span></i>
<br />
<div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
<a href="https://4.bp.blogspot.com/-cWqqhNWc1A8/VsCtJGcZESI/AAAAAAAABM4/rHYf69-ZGic/s1600/Antonin_Scalia%252C_SCOTUS_photo_portrait%2B-%2BPENCIL.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;"><img border="0" height="400" src="https://4.bp.blogspot.com/-cWqqhNWc1A8/VsCtJGcZESI/AAAAAAAABM4/rHYf69-ZGic/s400/Antonin_Scalia%252C_SCOTUS_photo_portrait%2B-%2BPENCIL.jpg" width="319" /></a></div>
<div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
<span style="color: #a2c4c9; font-family: &quot;courier new&quot; , &quot;courier&quot; , monospace; font-size: xx-small;">After Steve Pettway</span></div>
<i><span style="color: #45818e; font-family: &quot;trebuchet ms&quot; , sans-serif; font-size: large;"><br /></span></i>

</div>
<div class='post-body entry-content' id='post-body-7700968255062688588' itemprop='description articleBody'>
<i><span style="color: #45818e; font-family: &quot;trebuchet ms&quot; , sans-serif; font-size: large;">Join Mountain Rescue</span></i><br />
<i><span style="color: #45818e; font-family: &quot;trebuchet ms&quot; , sans-serif; font-size: large;">Home a rescue mountain now!</span></i><br />
<i><span style="color: #45818e; font-family: &quot;trebuchet ms&quot; , sans-serif; font-size: large;">"A knoll is for life..."</span></i><br />

<span style="color: #45818e; font-family: &quot;trebuchet ms&quot; , sans-serif; font-size: x-small;">or do you prefer</span><br />
<i><span style="color: #45818e; font-family: &quot;trebuchet ms&quot; , sans-serif; font-size: large;"><br /></span></i>
<i><span style="color: #45818e; font-family: &quot;trebuchet ms&quot; , sans-serif; font-size: large;">Join Mountain Rescue</span></i><br />
<i><span style="color: #45818e; font-family: &quot;trebuchet ms&quot; , sans-serif; font-size: large;">Home a rescue mountain now!</span></i><br />
<i><span style="color: #45818e; font-family: &quot;trebuchet ms&quot; , sans-serif; font-size: large;">"A troll is for life..."</span></i><br />

<h2 class='date-header'><span>31.1.16</span></h2>

          <div class="date-posts">
        
<div class='post-outer'>
<div class='post hentry uncustomized-post-template' itemprop='blogPost' itemscope='itemscope' itemtype='http://schema.org/BlogPosting'>
<meta content='http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-xXLEkffMwWY/Vq3kbejG37I/AAAAAAAABKI/nx1GI08EOoU/s1600/Happy_moose.jpg' itemprop='image_url'/>
<meta content='275300702743490151' itemprop='blogId'/>
<meta content='8553453319348689494' itemprop='postId'/>
<a name='8553453319348689494'></a>
<h3 class='post-title entry-title' itemprop='name'>
<a href='http://daikupcj.blogspot.com/2016/01/echo-chamber-music.html'>Echo Chamber Music</a>
</h3>
<div class='post-header'>
<div class='post-header-line-1'></div>
</div>
<div class='post-body entry-content' id='post-body-8553453319348689494' itemprop='description articleBody'>
<span style="color: #45818e; font-family: &quot;trebuchet ms&quot; , sans-serif;"><i><span style="font-size: x-large;">Moose!</span><span style="font-size: large;"> Moose! </span>Moose!<span style="font-size: x-small;"> Moose! </span><span style="font-size: xx-small;">Moose!</span></i></span><br />
<span style="color: #45818e; font-family: &quot;trebuchet ms&quot; , sans-serif;"><i><span style="font-size: x-large;">Caboose!</span><span style="font-size: large;"> Caboose! </span>Caboose!<span style="font-size: large;"> </span><span style="font-size: x-small;">'oose!</span></i></span><br />
<span style="color: #45818e; font-family: &quot;trebuchet ms&quot; , sans-serif; font-size: large;"><i>Dialed the reverb down</i></span><br />
<span style="color: #45818e; font-family: &quot;trebuchet ms&quot; , sans-serif; font-size: large;"><i><br /></i></span>
<span style="color: #45818e; font-family: &quot;trebuchet ms&quot; , sans-serif; font-size: x-small;"><i>or do you prefer</i></span><br />
<span style="color: #45818e; font-family: &quot;trebuchet ms&quot; , sans-serif; font-size: large;"><i><br /></i></span>
<span style="color: #45818e; font-family: &quot;trebuchet ms&quot; , sans-serif;"><i><span style="font-size: x-large;">Moose!</span><span style="font-size: large;"> Moose! </span>Moose! <span style="font-size: x-small;">Moose!</span><span style="font-size: large;"> </span><span style="font-size: xx-small;">Moose!</span></i></span><br />
<span style="color: #45818e; font-family: &quot;trebuchet ms&quot; , sans-serif;"><i><span style="font-size: x-large;">Caboose! </span><span style="font-size: large;">Caboose! </span>'oose! Moose! Loose!</i></span><br />
<span style="color: #45818e; font-family: &quot;trebuchet ms&quot; , sans-serif; font-size: large;"><i>Turned the echo off</i></span><br />
<span style="color: #45818e; font-family: &quot;trebuchet ms&quot; , sans-serif; font-size: large;"><i><br /></i></span>
<span style="color: #45818e; font-family: &quot;trebuchet ms&quot; , sans-serif; font-size: large;"><i><br /></i></span>
<br />
<div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
<a href="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-xXLEkffMwWY/Vq3kbejG37I/AAAAAAAABKI/nx1GI08EOoU/s1600/Happy_moose.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;"><img border="0" src="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-xXLEkffMwWY/Vq3kbejG37I/AAAAAAAABKI/nx1GI08EOoU/s1600/Happy_moose.jpg" /></a></div>
<div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
<span style="color: #a2c4c9; font-family: &quot;courier new&quot; , &quot;courier&quot; , monospace; font-size: xx-small;">Credit: http://uncyclopedia.wikia.com/wiki/File:Happy_moose.jpg</span></div>
<span style="color: #45818e; font-family: &quot;trebuchet ms&quot; , sans-serif; font-size: large;"><i><br /></i></span>

<h3 class='post-title entry-title' itemprop='name'>
<a href='http://daikupcj.blogspot.com/2016/01/unintended-consequences.html'>Unintended Consequences</a>
</h3>
<div class='post-header'>
<div class='post-header-line-1'></div>
</div>
<div class='post-body entry-content' id='post-body-4406209270906433750' itemprop='description articleBody'>
<i><span style="color: #45818e; font-family: Trebuchet MS, sans-serif; font-size: large;">Parsee protection</span></i><br />
<i><span style="color: #45818e; font-family: Trebuchet MS, sans-serif; font-size: large;">Forbidding marrying out</span></i><br />
<i><span style="color: #45818e; font-family: Trebuchet MS, sans-serif; font-size: large;">Has contra-effect</span></i>

<div class='post-header'>
<div class='post-header-line-1'></div>
</div>
<div class='post-body entry-content' id='post-body-7347144444635643524' itemprop='description articleBody'>
<i><span style="color: #674ea7; font-family: &quot;trebuchet ms&quot; , sans-serif; font-size: large;">Dr Seuss</span></i><br />
<i><span style="color: #674ea7; font-family: &quot;trebuchet ms&quot; , sans-serif; font-size: large;">Once rode with a moose in a caboose</span></i><br />
<i><span style="color: #674ea7; font-family: &quot;trebuchet ms&quot; , sans-serif; font-size: large;">Alongside two unicorns</span></i><br />

<h2 class='date-header'><span>15.1.16</span></h2>

          <div class="date-posts">
        
<div class='post-outer'>
<div class='post hentry uncustomized-post-template' itemprop='blogPost' itemscope='itemscope' itemtype='http://schema.org/BlogPosting'>
<meta content='http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-hxeE0D1UQM8/VppHpR4EavI/AAAAAAAABJk/E-kb5b07iiI/s400/Richard-strauss-and-pauline-and-franz-1910%2B%25281%2529.jpg' itemprop='image_url'/>

<h3 class='post-title entry-title' itemprop='name'>
<a href='http://daikupcj.blogspot.com/2016/01/romantic-scoring.html'>Romantic Scoring</a>
</h3>
<div class='post-header'>
<div class='post-header-line-1'></div>
</div>
<div class='post-body entry-content' id='post-body-6879249978950149906' itemprop='description articleBody'>
<i><span style="color: #674ea7; font-family: &quot;helvetica neue&quot; , &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif; font-size: large;">Richard Strauss</span></i><br />
<span style="color: #674ea7; font-family: &quot;helvetica neue&quot; , &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif; font-size: large;"><i>Would've scored </i>Die Fledermaus</span><br />
<i><span style="color: #674ea7; font-family: &quot;helvetica neue&quot; , &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif; font-size: large;">For an ultrasonic soprano</span></i><br />
<i><span style="color: #674ea7; font-family: &quot;helvetica neue&quot; , &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif; font-size: large;">And her sunshine-shrinking beau.</span></i><br />
<i><span style="color: #674ea7; font-family: &quot;helvetica neue&quot; , &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif; font-size: large;"><br /></span></i>
<br />
<div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
<a href="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-hxeE0D1UQM8/VppHpR4EavI/AAAAAAAABJk/E-kb5b07iiI/s1600/Richard-strauss-and-pauline-and-franz-1910%2B%25281%2529.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;"><img border="0" height="342" src="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-hxeE0D1UQM8/VppHpR4EavI/AAAAAAAABJk/E-kb5b07iiI/s400/Richard-strauss-and-pauline-and-franz-1910%2B%25281%2529.jpg" width="400" /></a></div>
<div style="text-align: center;">
<i><span style="color: #b4a7d6; font-family: &quot;courier new&quot; , &quot;courier&quot; , monospace; font-size: xx-small;"><br /></span></i></div>
<div style="text-align: center;">
<i><span style="color: #b4a7d6; font-family: &quot;courier new&quot; , &quot;courier&quot; , monospace; font-size: xx-small;">Richard Strauss, Pauline and Franz Strauss, 1910</span></i></div>
<div style="text-align: center;">

<h3 class='post-title entry-title' itemprop='name'>

</h3>
<div class='post-header'>
<div class='post-header-line-1'></div>
</div>
<div class='post-body entry-content' id='post-body-8112118703781156324' itemprop='description articleBody'>
<i><span style="color: #45818e; font-family: Trebuchet MS, sans-serif; font-size: large;">Poor conflicted sleuth</span></i><br />
<i><span style="color: #45818e; font-family: Trebuchet MS, sans-serif; font-size: large;">Improvised explosive vice</span></i><br />
<i><span style="color: #45818e; font-family: Trebuchet MS, sans-serif; font-size: large;">In his Mined Palace</span></i><br />
<i><span style="color: #45818e; font-family: Trebuchet MS, sans-serif; font-size: large;"><br /></span></i>
<br />
<div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
<a href="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-30Az9w5jG5U/VpLqjaVe4II/AAAAAAAABJU/4-MnT_Yw3BM/s1600/M-T-Cicero.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;"><img border="0" height="320" src="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-30Az9w5jG5U/VpLqjaVe4II/AAAAAAAABJU/4-MnT_Yw3BM/s320/M-T-Cicero.jpg" width="213" /></a></div>
<div style="text-align: center;">
<span style="color: #45818e; font-family: 'Courier New', Courier, monospace; font-size: xx-small;">"M-T-Cicero" by Gunnar Bach Pedersen; Image&nbsp;</span><span style="color: #45818e; font-family: 'Courier New', Courier, monospace; font-size: xx-small;">&#169;&nbsp;</span><span style="color: #45818e; font-family: 'Courier New', Courier, monospace; font-size: xx-small;">Thorvaldsen</span></div>

<h2 class='date-header'><span>6.1.16</span></h2>

          <div class="date-posts">
        
<div class='post-outer'>
<div class='post hentry uncustomized-post-template' itemprop='blogPost' itemscope='itemscope' itemtype='http://schema.org/BlogPosting'>
<meta content='275300702743490151' itemprop='blogId'/>
<meta content='5798383044715242477' itemprop='postId'/>
<a name='5798383044715242477'></a>
<h3 class='post-title entry-title' itemprop='name'>
<a href='http://daikupcj.blogspot.com/2016/01/dementia-is-not-female-dementor.html'>Dementia is not a female Dementor...</a>
</h3>
<div class='post-header'>
<div class='post-header-line-1'></div>
</div>
<div class='post-body entry-content' id='post-body-5798383044715242477' itemprop='description articleBody'>
<i><span style="color: #45818e; font-family: Trebuchet MS, sans-serif; font-size: large;">Illness eats ego</span></i><br />
<i><span style="color: #45818e; font-family: Trebuchet MS, sans-serif; font-size: large;">Shrunken frame; skin of parchment</span></i><br />
<i><span style="color: #45818e; font-family: Trebuchet MS, sans-serif; font-size: large;">That Great Brain Robber</span></i>

          <div class="date-posts">
        
<div class='post-outer'>
<div class='post hentry uncustomized-post-template' itemprop='blogPost' itemscope='itemscope' itemtype='http://schema.org/BlogPosting'>
<meta content='http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-BXqIWiZlLb4/VopAauRLGZI/AAAAAAAABHs/GKP8DG4ApUw/s400/Steven%2BPinker%2BSense%2Bof%2BStyle%2BFC150.jpg' itemprop='image_url'/>
<meta content='275300702743490151' itemprop='blogId'/>

<h3 class='post-title entry-title' itemprop='name'>
<a href='http://daikupcj.blogspot.com/2016/01/homo-grammariens.html'>Homo Grammariens</a>
</h3>
<div class='post-header'>
<div class='post-header-line-1'></div>
</div>
<div class='post-body entry-content' id='post-body-1712296252437372186' itemprop='description articleBody'>
<i><span style="color: #674ea7; font-family: Helvetica Neue, Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif; font-size: large;">Steven Pinker.</span></i><br />
<i><span style="color: #674ea7; font-family: Helvetica Neue, Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif; font-size: large;">Linguistically challenging thinker.</span></i><br />
<i><span style="color: #674ea7; font-family: Helvetica Neue, Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif; font-size: large;">Bringing us down from the case trees,</span></i><br />
<i><span style="color: #674ea7; font-family: Helvetica Neue, Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif; font-size: large;">The rich savannas of grammar to seize.</span></i><br />
<br />
<div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
</div>
<br />
<div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
<a href="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-BXqIWiZlLb4/VopAauRLGZI/AAAAAAAABHs/GKP8DG4ApUw/s1600/Steven%2BPinker%2BSense%2Bof%2BStyle%2BFC150.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;"><img border="0" height="400" src="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-BXqIWiZlLb4/VopAauRLGZI/AAAAAAAABHs/GKP8DG4ApUw/s400/Steven%2BPinker%2BSense%2Bof%2BStyle%2BFC150.jpg" width="257" /></a></div>

          <div class="date-posts">
        
<div class='post-outer'>
<div class='post hentry uncustomized-post-template' itemprop='blogPost' itemscope='itemscope' itemtype='http://schema.org/BlogPosting'>
<meta content='http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-Qeg4Sf6jEWI/VoiJdU2fVNI/AAAAAAAABHU/hTsyKsxJxuI/s400/Pink%2BAR-15.JPG' itemprop='image_url'/>
<meta content='275300702743490151' itemprop='blogId'/>

<a name='6984058023882756242'></a>
<h3 class='post-title entry-title' itemprop='name'>
<a href='http://daikupcj.blogspot.com/2016/01/no-five-minute-argument.html'>No Five Minute Argument...</a>
</h3>
<div class='post-header'>
<div class='post-header-line-1'></div>
</div>
<div class='post-body entry-content' id='post-body-6984058023882756242' itemprop='description articleBody'>
<i><span style="color: #45818e; font-family: Trebuchet MS, sans-serif; font-size: large;">There are none so deaf</span></i><br />
<i><span style="color: #45818e; font-family: Trebuchet MS, sans-serif; font-size: large;">As those who're wilfully blind</span></i><br />
<i><span style="color: #45818e; font-family: Trebuchet MS, sans-serif; font-size: large;">Beam and mote and eye</span></i><br />
<i><span style="color: #45818e; font-family: Trebuchet MS, sans-serif; font-size: large;"><br /></span></i>
<div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
<a href="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-Qeg4Sf6jEWI/VoiJdU2fVNI/AAAAAAAABHU/hTsyKsxJxuI/s1600/Pink%2BAR-15.JPG" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;"><img border="0" height="153" src="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-Qeg4Sf6jEWI/VoiJdU2fVNI/AAAAAAAABHU/hTsyKsxJxuI/s400/Pink%2BAR-15.JPG" width="400" /></a></div>
<i><span style="color: #45818e; font-family: Trebuchet MS, sans-serif; font-size: large;"><br /></span></i>

<div class='post-body entry-content' id='post-body-1154576650119726277' itemprop='description articleBody'>
<i><span style="color: #45818e; font-family: Trebuchet MS, sans-serif; font-size: large;">To quaff not to sip</span></i><br />
<i><span style="color: #45818e; font-family: Trebuchet MS, sans-serif; font-size: large;">Curries' perfect counterpoint</span></i><br />
<i><span style="color: #45818e; font-family: Trebuchet MS, sans-serif; font-size: large;">India Pail Ale</span></i><br />

<h2 class='date-header'><span>22.12.15</span></h2>

          <div class="date-posts">
        
<div class='post-outer'>
<div class='post hentry uncustomized-post-template' itemprop='blogPost' itemscope='itemscope' itemtype='http://schema.org/BlogPosting'>
<meta content='http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-IAl8vmANYFc/Vnp2xj9QM2I/AAAAAAAABGU/gVRjuYu94Ug/s400/Falstaff_rebuked_%2528Smirke%252C_c._1795%2529%2B%255BCropped%255D.jpg' itemprop='image_url'/>
<meta content='275300702743490151' itemprop='blogId'/>
<meta content='8973870110113197605' itemprop='postId'/>
<a name='8973870110113197605'></a>
<h3 class='post-title entry-title' itemprop='name'>
<a href='http://daikupcj.blogspot.com/2015/12/prince-harry.html'>Prince Harry</a>
</h3>
<div class='post-header'>
<div class='post-header-line-1'></div>
</div>
<div class='post-body entry-content' id='post-body-8973870110113197605' itemprop='description articleBody'>
<i><span style="color: #45818e; font-family: Trebuchet MS, sans-serif; font-size: large;">Any doubts about</span></i><br />
<i><span style="color: #45818e; font-family: Trebuchet MS, sans-serif; font-size: large;">The Tudors' Welsh roots would've made</span></i><br />
<i><span style="color: #45818e; font-family: Trebuchet MS, sans-serif; font-size: large;">Henry a false Taff</span></i><br />
<i><span style="color: #45818e; font-family: Trebuchet MS, sans-serif; font-size: large;"><br /></span></i>
<br />
<div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
<a href="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-IAl8vmANYFc/Vnp2xj9QM2I/AAAAAAAABGU/gVRjuYu94Ug/s1600/Falstaff_rebuked_%2528Smirke%252C_c._1795%2529%2B%255BCropped%255D.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;"><img border="0" height="347" src="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-IAl8vmANYFc/Vnp2xj9QM2I/AAAAAAAABGU/gVRjuYu94Ug/s400/Falstaff_rebuked_%2528Smirke%252C_c._1795%2529%2B%255BCropped%255D.jpg" width="400" /></a></div>
<div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
<span style="color: #a2c4c9; font-family: Courier New, Courier, monospace; font-size: xx-small;">Falstaff Rebuked, Smirke (c. 1795)</span></div>
<br />
<div style='clear: both;'></div>
</div>

          <div class="date-posts">
        
<div class='post-outer'>
<div class='post hentry uncustomized-post-template' itemprop='blogPost' itemscope='itemscope' itemtype='http://schema.org/BlogPosting'>
<meta content='http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-3ta5YSoLmXA/VnIL-0YmXLI/AAAAAAAABCA/b-E4v_r2C1M/s400/640px-Molon_labe.jpg' itemprop='image_url'/>
<meta content='275300702743490151' itemprop='blogId'/>

<h3 class='post-title entry-title' itemprop='name'>
<a href='http://daikupcj.blogspot.com/2015/12/totemic-polemic.html'>Totemic Polemic</a>
</h3>
<div class='post-header'>
<div class='post-header-line-1'></div>
</div>
<div class='post-body entry-content' id='post-body-8918360313338653082' itemprop='description articleBody'>
<i><span style="color: #674ea7; font-family: &quot;helvetica neue&quot; , &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif; font-size: large;">Americans' Superheroes.</span></i><br />
<div>
<i><span style="color: #674ea7; font-family: &quot;helvetica neue&quot; , &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif; font-size: large;">Sorting the World's woes.</span></i></div>
<div>
<i><span style="color: #674ea7; font-family: &quot;helvetica neue&quot; , &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif; font-size: large;">Though hogs might fly,</span></i></div>
<div>
<i><span style="color: #674ea7; font-family: &quot;helvetica neue&quot; , &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif; font-size: large;">Before they'd cheer for Gun Control Guy.</span></i></div>
<div>
<i><span style="color: #674ea7; font-family: &quot;helvetica neue&quot; , &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif; font-size: large;"><br /></span></i></div>
<div>
<span style="color: #674ea7; font-family: &quot;helvetica neue&quot; , &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif; font-size: x-small;">Or do you like</span></div>
<div>
<i><span style="color: #674ea7; font-family: &quot;helvetica neue&quot; , &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif; font-size: large;"><br /></span></i></div>
<div>
<i><span style="color: #674ea7; font-family: &quot;helvetica neue&quot; , &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif; font-size: large;">America's Superheroes.</span></i><br />
<div>
<i><span style="color: #674ea7; font-family: &quot;helvetica neue&quot; , &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif; font-size: large;">Sorting the World's woes.</span></i></div>
<div>
<i><span style="color: #674ea7; font-family: &quot;helvetica neue&quot; , &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif; font-size: large;">The one Superhero bound to turn necks red?</span></i></div>
<div>
<i><span style="color: #674ea7; font-family: &quot;helvetica neue&quot; , &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif; font-size: large;">Background Checking Fed.</span></i></div>
